            let vault_root = active_vault.read(cx).config.root.clone();
            let note_path = note_path_for_target(&vault_root, target)?;
            if !note_path.exists() {
                if let Some(parent) = note_path.parent() {
                    if let Err(err) = std::fs::create_dir_all(parent) {
                        log::error!("Oxidian: failed to create note directory {parent:?}: {err}");
                        return None;
                    }
                }
                let title = note_path
                    .file_stem()
                    .and_then(|stem| stem.to_str())
                    .unwrap_or(target);
                if let Err(err) = std::fs::write(&note_path, format!("# {title}\n\n")) {
                    log::error!("Oxidian: failed to create note {note_path:?}: {err}");
                    return None;
                }
            }

```

fn calendar_cells(year: i32, month: u32) -> Vec<(NaiveDate, bool)> {
    let Some(first_day) = NaiveDate::from_ymd_opt(year, month, 1) else {
        return Vec::new();
    };

    let weekday_num = first_day.weekday().number_from_monday();
    let prev_month_days = weekday_num - 1;

    let (prev_year, prev_month) = if month == 1 {
        (year - 1, 12)
    } else {
        (year, month - 1)
    };
    let prev_month_len = days_in_month(prev_year, prev_month);

    let mut cells = Vec::with_capacity(42);

    for i in (0..prev_month_days).rev() {
        let day = prev_month_len - i;
        if let Some(date) = NaiveDate::from_ymd_opt(prev_year, prev_month, day) {
            cells.push((date, false));
        }
    }

    let current_month_len = days_in_month(year, month);
    for day in 1..=current_month_len {
        if let Some(date) = NaiveDate::from_ymd_opt(year, month, day) {
            cells.push((date, true));
        }
    }

    let remaining = 42usize.saturating_sub(cells.len());
    let (next_year, next_month) = if month == 12 {
        (year + 1, 1)
    } else {
        (year, month + 1)
    };
    for day in 1..=remaining {
        if let Some(date) = NaiveDate::from_ymd_opt(next_year, next_month, day as u32) {
            cells.push((date, false));
        }
    }

    cells
}

Diff: /home/julesklord/Proyectos/repos/oxidian/crates/oxidian_frontmatter/src/oxidian_frontmatter.rs
```
fn find_frontmatter_range(text: &str) -> Option<std::ops::Range<usize>> {
    let delimiter = if text.starts_with("---\r\n") {
        "\r\n"
    } else if text.starts_with("---\n") {
        "\n"
    } else {
        return None;
    };

    let start_len = 3 + delimiter.len();
    if let Some(end_offset) = text[start_len..].find(&format!("---{delimiter}")) {
        let end_abs = start_len + end_offset + 3 + delimiter.len();
        return Some(0..end_abs);
    }

    None

```


Diff: /home/julesklord/Proyectos/repos/oxidian/crates/oxidian_frontmatter/src/oxidian_frontmatter.rs
```

fn is_valid_property_key(key: &str) -> bool {
    !key.is_empty()
        && key
            .chars()
            .all(|ch| ch.is_ascii_alphanumeric() || matches!(ch, '_' | '-'))
}

Try calling update() first\")\n    }\n\n    fn read_entity<T, R>(&self, handle: &Entity<T>, callback: impl FnOnce(&T, &App) -> R) -> R\n    where\n        T: 'static,\n    {\n        let app = self.app();\n        let lock = app.borrow();\n        lock.read_entity(handle, callback)\n    }\n\n    fn update_window<T, F>(&mut self, window: AnyWindowHandle, f: F) -> Result<T>\n    where\n        F: FnOnce(AnyView, &mut Window, &mut App) -> T,\n    {\n        let app = self.app.upgrade().context(\"app was released\")?;\n        let mut lock = app.try_borrow_mut()?;\n        if lock.quitting {\n            bail!(\"app is quitting\");\n        }\n        lock.update_window(window, f)\n    }\n\n    fn with_window<R>(\n        &mut self,\n        entity_id: EntityId,\n        f: impl ## Assistant

La primera validación encontró un detalle de API de GPUI: `detach_and_log_err` requiere `&App`, pero el watcher corre con `AsyncApp`. Lo cambio por un wrapper explícito que espera la tarea y registra el error, compatible con ese contexto.
